5. **Final Calculation**:
- Complete the remaining operations from left to right.
- 628 - 1 = 627.

- fa = -3
- f'a = -31

Concatenation of fa and f'a is -3-31 = -34.

However, due to the new operation of primefactor, which counts the unique prime factors common to two numbers, we need to consider the prime factors of -3 and -31.

- Prime factors of -3 are 3 and -1.
- Prime factors of -31 are 31 and -1.

The only shared prime factor is -1, so primefactor(-3#-31) = -1.

Finally, we apply the new operation of sub, which subtracts the second number from the first number.

- (-3#-31)#-1 = -34#-1 = -33.

**Solution:**

1. **Parentheses:**

Evaluate the expression inside the parentheses first:

14 + 4 = 18

2. **Concatenation:**

Concatenate 6 with 18:

6 @ 18 = 618

3. **Addition:**

Add 618 and 12:

618 + 12 = 630

4. **Prime Factor Counting:**

Determine the number of unique prime factors shared by 630 and 3:

630 = 2 * 3^2 * 5 * 7
3 = 3

The only shared prime factor is 3, so 630#3 = 1.

5. **Subtraction:**

Subtract 1 from 630:

630 - 1 = 629

- 630 - 0 = 630

- Perform concatenation again.

- Perform addition next.
- 618 + 12 = 630

- Prime factors of 3 are 3.
- The only shared prime factor is 3, so 630#3 = 1.

- Perform subtraction last.
- 630 - 1 = 629

**The answer is 629.**		 1. **Prime Factor Counting (F):** We start by calculating the count of unique prime factors shared between the absolute values of 2 and 3.
- |2| = 2, prime factors: {2}
- |3| = 3, prime factors: {3}
- Shared prime factors: {}
- 2#3 = 0 (since there are no shared prime factors)


2. **Parentheses:** We evaluate the expression inside the parentheses first.
- 14 + 4 = 18


3. **Concatenation (C):** Next, we perform the concatenation operation.
- 6 @ (14 + 4) = 6 @ 18 = 618


4. **Addition:** We add the results of the previous steps.
- 618 + 12 = 630


5. **Subtraction:** Finally, we subtract 2#3 from the result of the previous step.

- 108 + 12 - 2 = 120 - 2 = 118

Given:


[(5^3 + 2^4) * 100] - [4500 + (60 * 6)] = ?



Using the new order of operations, we have:


1. Evaluate expressions within parentheses first.
[Parentheses]
Exponents
Prime Factor
Concatenation
Multiplication/Division Left to Right
Subtraction/Addition Left to Right
2. Evaluate exponents and prime factorization.
[Exponents]
Prime Factor
Concatenation
Multiplication/Division Left to Right
Subtraction/Addition Left to Right
3. Perform Concatenation
4. Perform multiplication and division from left to right.
5. Perform subtraction and addition from left to right.


Following these steps, we can evaluate the given expression:


[(5^3 + 2^4) * 100] - [4500 + (60 * 6)]

[125+16)*100]-[4500+(360)]

[141*100]-[4500+360]

[14100]-[4860]



The answer is 9240.


In this example, we need to evaluate the exponents and prime factorization, perform multiplication and division from left to right, and then perform subtraction and addition from left to right to find the final answer.

1. Parentheses
2. Exponents
3. Prime Factor Counting
4. Multiplication/Division (left to right)

6. Concatenation (left to right)

3. No multiplication or division to evaluate

The answer is 2.		 The answer is (10a^10bc^12d^13)^2.

Step-by-step solution:

First, we can simplify the expression using the laws of exponents.

(10a^10bc^12d^13)^2 = 10^2 * a^(10*2) * b^(c*2) * d^(13*2)

Then, we can simplify further by evaluating the powers.

10^2 = 100
a^(10*2) = a^20
b^(c*2) = b^c^2
d^(13*2) = d^26

Substituting these values back into the original expression, we get:

(10a^10bc^12d^13)^2 = 100 * a^20 * b^c^2 * d^26

Finally, we can simplify the expression one last time by multiplying the coefficients and combining the exponents.

100 * a^20 * b^c^2 * d^26 = (10a^10bc^12d^13)^2

Therefore, the answer is (10a^10bc^12d^13)^2.		 **Problem:** 8 # 2 + 6 # 6
